 CBI investigation is going on against the mining minister Gayatri Prajapati on the order of the High Court
 sarkaar ne sibiai jaanch na karaane ke liye hoicourt se darkhwaast kii thi jo hoicourt ne naamanzoor kar di
 The court asked for a status report soon
 iske baad sarkaar ko gayatri prajapati ko barkhaast karnaa padaa

 rajya main jald hi chunaav hone vaale hai
